Compilation of Military Reports from Various Parties 13

(Nanjing) The Capital Garrison Headquarters announced military news on the 19th: (1) After the rebellious enemy on the Longhai Line was bravely repelled by our army, enemy corpses were scattered everywhere, and the rebellious army collapsed towards Kaifeng. Our army took advantage of the victory to pursue and kill them. The elite of the enemy suffered heavy casualties and no longer had the ability to resist. Feng's entire army had a plan to withdraw to Zhengzhou and Luoyang. It is expected that they will meet in Zhengzhou soon. (2) The remnants of the rebellious enemy on the Longhai Line were shocked after hearing that our army had recovered Jinan. They still tried to attack us, hoping to achieve something. After being severely attacked by our army for days, only a few remnants remained, and they were out of ammunition and food and could not be replenished. They repeatedly tried to escape without success and are now only lurking in their positions with no combat ability. They will be completely annihilated within days. (3) Our air force has been bombing the enemy's positions for days, killing countless enemies. Ji Hongchang and An Shude were both injured in the bombing. An Shude was seriously injured and died immediately. His troops completely collapsed. The enemy troops are now extremely shaken and are in a state of great chaos. (4) Liu Zhennian's army in Jiaodong has advanced towards Boxing and Qingcheng. Liu himself is supervising the battle in Yexian, with morale at its peak, determined to destroy the enemy. They are now working with other friendly forces to cross the river and pursue the remaining enemies, meeting in Tianjin and Beijing. (5) On the Pinghan front, Wang Zhen's rebellious troops and the remnants of Wan Xuancai's troops have been fighting fiercely over occupying defensive positions and collecting supplies. They are now building fortifications and guarding against each other, and will not stop until both sides are badly damaged. (6) According to reports, our army has surrounded the enemy in Yongcheng on all sides. The city is running out of food, and many civilians are being released every day. Huang Xuchu's troops, about three regiments, came from Liuzhou to rescue Yongcheng and arrived in eastern Yongcheng, but were defeated by our army. The remnants fled to Liuzhou. Yongcheng is expected to be taken soon. (19th Special Telegram)

Weihaiwei Will Be Managed by a Commissioner 14

The Executive Yuan designates it as a naval port.

(Nanjing) Regarding the management of Weihaiwei after its recovery, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, together with the Ministries of Interior, Navy, Transportation, and Finance, held a meeting to review the matter and agreed on three options: (1) If the Central Government decides to immediately make Weihaiwei a naval port after its recovery, all facilities should be handled in accordance with military plans. (2) If, due to diplomatic, financial, or other issues, Weihaiwei cannot be immediately made a naval port after its recovery, then during the transition period, a special commissioner may be appointed by the Central Government to manage it. (3) If the second option is deemed inappropriate in the administrative system, then the only option is to follow the provisions of Article 2, Section 3 of the City Organization Law recently promulgated by the National Government and establish a city directly under the Executive Yuan, striving for simplicity and frugality in personnel organization to facilitate management and development. As for the establishment of a customs office, the allocation of office space, and the management of lighthouses, the review concluded that the establishment of a customs office and the allocation of office space were not a problem. However, the management of lighthouses, if it is made a naval port, should be classified as a military agency, otherwise it should be handled in accordance with the current methods of various ports. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has submitted the results of the above review to the Executive Yuan for review, and it is heard that the Executive Yuan plans to adopt the second option, designating Weihaiwei as a naval port and appointing a commissioner from the Central Government to manage it. After the matter is submitted to the government for decision, it will be promulgated. (10th and 9th Special Telegrams)

The Ministry of Finance Repoints Chinese Directors of the Sino-French Bank 15

(Nanjing) After the Sino-French Industrial Bank closed down, the Sino-French Industrial and Commercial Bank was established with a capital of 30 million francs. The old government of our country recognized one-third of it and allocated it from the US dollar bonds issued under the German returned indemnity. When the old government invested, it was agreed with the bank that the Chinese government, as a shareholder, could recommend seven people from the 21 directors of the bank, and could designate one person as vice chairman and one person as Chinese general manager, and select one person from the two supervisors of the bank. The above personnel have been successively appointed by the old government and the National Government. In order to exercise shareholder rights and enhance Sino-French relations, it is specially requested that Zhu Chengzhang and Li Chengyi be appointed to replace Li Guangqi and Su Yuchun as directors of the bank, and that Zeng Rongfu be appointed to replace the supervisor, and that Qian Yongming concurrently serve as the vice chairman of the bank in addition to his original position as Chinese general manager. (19th Special Telegram)

Zhang Xiangyun's Announcement: The Shandong Guild Hall in Shanghai reorganized in 1928 after the old board of directors stepped down, creating a Provisional Committee. Xiangyun was then invited by the Guild Hall to serve as an advisor, handling all diplomatic affairs, purely on a voluntary basis, without using any public funds. This can be reported without fault to all. In 1929, some Shandong natives in Shanghai formed the East Shandong Association, which then became embroiled in a dispute with the Shandong Guild Hall Committee, resulting in litigation. Maintaining peace, Xiangyun dared not involve himself, but his earnest efforts at reconciliation proved futile, leaving Xiangyun unwilling to rashly interfere. As the Guild Hall inevitably incurred expenses due to the litigation, Xiangyun was not involved in any of it. Moreover, Xiangyun has never handled any financial matters of the Guild Hall, fearing misunderstandings. Therefore, this announcement is made to clarify the situation, hoping that fellow provincials, elders, brothers, and sisters will understand.

(Nanjing) The Second Training Division engaged in several fierce battles with the forces of Guo Zongfen, Guan Fuan, Sun Chu, and others, capturing over a thousand soldiers. Japanese Police on South Manchurian Railway Assault Mail Carrier 21

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications previously received a report from the Postal Bureau stating that postal carrier Zuo Zhaoxiang of the Liaoning District was disembarking at Wenguantun on the South Manchurian Railway when he was forcibly inspected and brutally assaulted by Japanese police, sustaining injuries all over his body and broken ribs. The Ministry immediately telegraphed the Postal Bureau to lodge a serious protest. A subsequent report indicates that the Japanese Police Chief personally visited the Postal Bureau to offer a formal apology. Regarding the demands made, including: 1. Medical expenses for the hospital treatment to be borne by the Japanese side; 2. Compensation to be provided to the injured postal carrier; 3. Expenses for hiring a replacement worker to be borne by the Japanese side; 4. Removal and legal punishment of the offending officer, all were agreed to. The Ministry has now instructed the Bureau to continue negotiations to ensure that the Japanese side guarantees that similar incidents will not occur again in the future to maintain postal service. (19th Dispatch)

Examination Committee Standing Committee Meeting Resolutions 22

(Nanjing) The Examination Committee of the Examination Yuan held its 23rd meeting on the 19th. (1) Regarding the "Regulations for Examination Verification," it was resolved that, except for Article 5, which was reserved for further review, the remaining articles were amended and passed. (2) Regarding the proposal from the First Group of Special Committee Members to request instructions on the preliminary key points for drafting the "Ordinary Examination Regulations," it was resolved that: 1. The format of the "Ordinary Examination Regulations" does not need to follow the classification of the Higher Examinations. It should be based on the similarities and differences in their nature, combining where possible, and drafting separately where not possible. 2. The qualification requirements for the Ordinary Examination, according to the provisions of the Examination Law, shall require graduation from secondary schools or above, with the interpretation of "secondary schools" limited to the new system's senior high schools, the old system's middle schools, and other equivalent schools. Those who have only graduated from junior high school must undergo a verification examination before being allowed to take the Ordinary Examination. (19th Dispatch)

International Important News

League of Nations Council Election: China Should Strive for a Seat 45

Geneva, 18th - National Society: In the League of Nations Council, three council seats will be up for election this year. Many are vying for these seats, and a fierce competition is expected. Currently, the terms of Cuba, Finland, and Canada are expiring. For Cuba's seat, several Latin American countries are competing, and it may be won by Guatemala. For Finland's seat, Norway is seeking election, arguing that this seat should remain with the Scandinavian countries. For Canada's seat, the likely contenders are China, the Union of South Africa, and Belgium. The Prime Minister of South Africa will personally attend the meetings in Geneva, which can be seen as an expression of seeking to be elected as a council member. The UK will support South Africa in the election, while France will support Belgium.

China Wins Top Awards

Liège Correspondence: The Belgian Exposition has organized an international awards competition to encourage exhibitors. Italy won the highest award for its electric trains. Japan did not exhibit much this time, but the exhibition hall was larger. Its silk fabrics and porcelain were not as exquisite as China's. China's exhibits, including tea, porcelain, cloisonné, carpets, silk, embroidery, and carvings, won the highest awards. In addition, the mulberry and silkworm specimens from the Agricultural College of Zhejiang University, the educational achievements of schools at all levels in various regions, and physical education equipment were admired by foreigners and also won awards. Hindenburg Declares Neutrality on Party Affairs

Schrecker Releases Steady Claims

Berlin, 18th - The German election campaign is progressing rapidly, with important events occurring daily. Recently, two significant events occurred. One was President Hindenburg's declaration, stating that he does not wish to be involved in any form of party affairs. Currently, there are elements of the National Right Wing organizing a Hindenburg group, calling for support for Hindenburg, hoping to gain public support. Therefore, the President issued this declaration to clarify the truth. The other event was the first speech by General Schrecker, the former German Commander-in-Chief, after becoming a candidate for the National Party. The outside world was quite suspicious of Schrecker's sudden entry into the political arena, suspecting that he harbored ambitions. Therefore, his speech began by declaring that he is already sixty-four years old and has long abandoned political ambitions. He believes that the current situation is critical, and as a citizen, he should do his best to find a solution and promote the development of parliamentary politics. Therefore, he came out to participate in politics to fulfill his duty as a citizen. However, no matter what, he will vigorously oppose all radical solutions because a radical government is like sailing a boat on a course with no definite destination. However, he strongly advocated cooperation with the Social Democratic Party because the demands of millions of workers in that party cannot be ignored. Finally, when discussing several important domestic issues, he expressed extremely steady claims.

British Colonial Enterprise 50

Unifying Official Duties

Establishing Regular Aviation

London, 18th - The Colonial Office issued a memorandum on the unification of colonial duties, stating that the principle of unifying colonial duties into one does not rely on the positive changes in the current situation. The committee studying the Colonial Office's personnel system and colonial duties clearly knows that officials serving in unified colonial duties acknowledge the possibility of being transferred from one colony to another during their tenure. After unifying colonial duties, the Colonial Secretary will have great opportunities to assign appropriate people to appropriate positions so that they can develop their experience. However, the so-called unification of duties does not mean that colonial officials will be transferred constantly, making their footprints all over the world. The unification of duties will definitely be of great benefit to the governments of various colonies.

London, 19th - According to the Blue Book issued by the Colonial Office Conference, after the "Flight K-100" and "R-101" have been test-flown several times and accumulated sufficient experience, the government will establish regular aviation services between Gaddington in the UK, Montreal in Canada, and New York in the US. There are approximately three main routes: (1) passing the Farewell Cape at the southern tip of Greenland; (2) passing Newfoundland; (3) passing the Azores Islands. In addition, there is another route, which is through the Faas Islands, Iceland, and the Herzog Bay of Greenland in the North Sea. This is the route currently being investigated by the expedition under the guidance of Hawkins. The Blue Book mentions the US plan to set up a seaplane airport every three hundred nautical miles between New York and the Azores, and between the Azores and Plymouth, to facilitate refueling and repairs.

It is extremely illegal and has been verified by the envoy, and all should be confiscated to rectify the salt regulations. Upon receiving this, I was shocked and at a loss. However, punishing corruption and greed was originally taught by the late Prime Minister and declared by the government. There is no need to start a major lawsuit, and reach the world's lesson of resolving matters and appeasing people. It is better to be heartbroken by corruption and arrogance and not allow consideration. I am forced to be here and have nowhere to escape. I hope that the Ministry will not cherish this horse that harms the people, so that it can punish one and warn a hundred, and serve as a warning to the world. The corruption of the political image is extremely serious. Tong Sheng is naturally strong and not afraid of the strong. Now, in order to promote the authority of the law, he has specially filed a lawsuit in the Qingdao Local Court where Chen Chen currently resides and committed the crime, revealing everything and vowing to pursue it to the end in order to demonstrate the law and discipline and warn the official evil. This is a telegram for your review. I beg you to advocate justice and do not fail to cut prayers. The Ji Yu Company representative Yin Tongsheng kowtows skillfully.

News Two

Central Army Captures Jinan and Crosses the River Northward 56

Armies on the Jiaoji Railway Line Meet to Pursue the Enemy

Feng's Army on the Longhai Railway Line Retreats Westward Under Pressure

Express mail from Xuzhou: The Central Army on the Jinpu Railway Line has made rapid progress. It reached Jinan on the 15th. It has been described in the previous letter. Now, according to the front news, Jinan has been completely occupied by the Central Army, and the advance troops have crossed the river northward. The armies on the Jiaoji Railway Line are meeting in Jinan, and Feng's army on the Longhai Railway Line is also retreating westward at the same time. The details are as follows:

Details of the Capture of Jinan: After the Jin army lost Tai'an, it had no power to resist. Although it deployed defenses near Jinan in an attempt to make a final struggle, it had already transported the military strength across the river. The Central Army still advanced fiercely from the left, right, and middle routes. On the 14th, the right wing, led by Jiang Guangnai and Cai Tingkai, broke through the Jin army at Dajiankou, 15 miles southeast of Jinan, and had already shaken Jinan. The middle route, led by Chen Cheng and Xia Douyin, advanced to Jiajiazhuang. The Jin army had no resistance. The left wing, led by Yang Shengzhi and the teaching division, flanked the northwest of Jinan, and the army had worries about the return route being cut off, so it had to retreat north in a hurry. At 2:00 PM on the 15th, Jiang and Cai's divisions first copied to Jinan from the right wing, and Chen and Xia's divisions in the middle route also arrived to join forces. Yang's division and the teaching divisions on the left wing had already copied the northwest of Jinan. The city of Jinan fell at that time. The Central Army all reorganized their divisions, cleaned up the remnants of the enemy in the city, and immediately sent troops to bypass the north to block the Yellow River Bridge in Luokou. The materials of the bridge had been dismantled by the Central Government before abandoning Jinan and transported to Bengbu for preservation. After the Jin army arrived in Jinan, they only built a temporary pontoon bridge for transportation. At this time, it was cut off by the Central Army again. The Jin army did not expect the Central Army to capture Jinan so quickly. Most of them did not have time to retreat north. About 10,000 people surrendered to the Central Government and handed over a large number of weapons. Liu Zhi, the commander-in-chief, had already arrived in Tai'an to supervise the army. At this time, he also left the Tai'an station on the 15th evening and went north to Jinan. The order in Jinan was greatly stabilized. However, when the Jin army retreated from the south of Jinan, they greatly damaged the roads. The Zhangxia Bridge was also destroyed. The road is being repaired temporarily. At this time, the remnants of the enemy in Tai'an, Feng Yuxi's troops, were also disarmed by the 15th Army Ma Tengjiao Division, and completely cleaned up. At present, the Central Army is continuing to clean up the remnants of the enemy on the south bank of the Yellow River, and sending troops to pursue the north. The following is an excerpt of the victory from the front received by Xu Xingying: (1) According to the airplane, our army captured Jinan at noon today, and the reverse enemy fled to Hebei. (2) According to the telegram from Commander-in-Chief Liu, our army has indeed occupied the city of Jinan at 2:00 PM today and sent troops to guard the Yellow River Iron Bridge. The enemy in Henan has no way to retreat and can be completely annihilated.

Meeting of Jiaoji Road: The Han Fuju, Liu Zhennian, and Li Yunheng units on the Jiaoji line are also actively advancing westward. Commander-in-Chief Han arrived at Tancheng Station on the 13th to supervise the attack on the enemy at Bailang River. The enemy army collapsed and the Han army pursued the troops. Then, they passed Changle and repaired the road westward along the way. At present, the return route of the Jin army on the Jiaoji line to Jinan has been cut off, and a part of the Jiang Guangnai division has cut off the road line from Boshan. It has withdrawn to the north of the road line and is collapsing to Hebei from the Boxing and Qingcheng areas. The clearing of the Jiaoji line is also very easy. Mr. Jiang Bocheng was ordered to plan military affairs with Han Fuju and also advanced westward with Han.

Longhai Army Advances Westward: The Feng army on the Longhai line, in order to aid the Jin army on the Jinpu line, has repeatedly counterattacked from the left wing, but they were all repelled. On the 14th night, Feng also ordered Song Zheyuan and Ji Hongchang to attack the Central Army's position. The Central Army was prepared and immediately counterattacked. Song and Ji were defeated. At present, the Jin army lost Jinan, and the Feng army collapsed westward overnight. The Central Army took the opportunity to advance and has crossed Minquan Neihuang and directly approached Lanfeng again, killing more than 10,000 enemy officers and soldiers. Now, they are pursuing from the left and right wings. Qiu Wei, the director of the transportation office of the general headquarters, sent a telegram to Xu from the west road yesterday to Director He Yaozu and Transportation Commander Qian Zongze, asking them to quickly prepare materials such as railway tracks, bridges, and electric poles, and transport them to the front overnight to follow the army for repairs and facilitate transportation. It is reported that Feng will implement the plan to abandon Bian and defend Zheng.

Generals Come to Xu: In the midst of the Jinan victory, Yang Jie was summoned by Jiang's telegram and came to Xu from Tai'an on the 15th evening and will go west. Yang met with Mr. He Yaozu in Xu to discuss everything. It was decided to take the same car west that night to report the Jinan situation and plan future military affairs. According to Li Jun, the chief of staff of Yang's fortress headquarters, our army has absolute certainty of winning Jinan. Yang came south from Tai'an this time, took a car to Nan Station, then took a car to Xu from Yan, and then went west with Director He to visit the main seat and plan other important matters. This morning, Ma Hongkui happened to return to Xu from Beijing to visit He Yang and decided to go west with him that night to report his official duties in Qingdao. (16th)

Hubei Provincial Army Begins to Suppress Bandits 57

Huayuan Xiaogan Guangshui Area Has Been Cleared

Correspondence from Hankou: Regarding the pacification of Hubei Province, the Wuhan camp has made specific arrangements in military affairs since the confirmation of the plan. Recently, powerful troops have been assembled on the Pinghan Line and the three sides of eastern, western, and southern Hubei to carry out the suppression. The operations began on the 16th. The following is a summary of the recent bandit suppression situation and the situation obtained by aircraft reconnaissance. The Huayuan Xiaogan Guangshui area on the Pinghan Road has many mountains and dense forests, and has always been an area where Communist bandits haunt. At the beginning of this month, a small number of Communist bandits often harassed various townships and towns, and sometimes even scurried to the vicinity of the railway, destroying rails and cutting off wires. Although Liu's regiment stationed in Huayuan of the 3rd Teaching Division repelled them, they were unable to pursue them due to their weak forces. Later, Dai Minquan of the New 25th Division led his troops to Hubei from Henan, and on the 14th and 15th, he joined forces with the 14th Independent Brigade and Liu's regiment to attack in different routes, killing many enemies. However, there are still more than 100 scattered remnants of bandits who are looting people in a certain village 30 miles away from Huayuan Station. They went to encircle and suppress them in the early morning of the 16th, killing more than 20 bandits, and the rest fled to the east. At present, the bandits in the Guangxiao area have been cleared. As for the bandits in Tonghaikou in western Hubei, Chen's camp of Liu's regiment also went to suppress them fiercely yesterday on the 17th, and sent a camp to intercept them by surprise in Pengjiaju. After a battle of about two hours, about 100 bandits were killed, more than a dozen earth guns and countless flags were seized. The bandits fled to Fengkou via Baimiao Makou. Today (18th), the 1st Aviation Team, led by Lu Zhenxian, flew to the Fengkou Mianyang Baimiao area at 5:30 in the morning to conduct reconnaissance in a new T克罗斯 aircraft. It was detected that the inside of Fengkou Village was extremely chaotic, and there were many small boats parked in the river, which seemed to be occupied by bandits. Two 120-pound bombs were dropped, and then the aircraft flew to the villages in Qingshankou Dongyanggang east of Xiaohaxi. There were also bandits stationed, and one bomb was dropped in Qingshankou, and the aircraft was lowered and strafed with machine guns, and another bomb was dropped in Gongjiamu. Tonghaikou, Mianyang, Xiadian, Caidian, Meidian, etc. were very quiet, and no traces of bandits were found. Zhang Yougu of the 1st Aviation Team also flew to the area of Wuxue Tianjiazhen Longpingzhen Huangmei Guangji in eastern Hubei to detect the traces of bandits. Only dozens of small boat bandits were found near Dajinpu, some holding guns, some holding red flags, and some holding knives and spears. A 120-pound bomb was given as a reward, killing more than a dozen bandits. All the large and small roads in the other counties have been carefully detected, and there are no traces of bandits. (August 18)

Post-Loot Donation in Hunan Province 58

Tax on Farmland Rents Ranging from 4% to 16%

Tax on Capital Ranging from 1% to 5%

Tax on Houses Ranging from 8‰ to 14‰

Changsha Correspondence: Hunan Province was ravaged by the Gui Zhang army in the recent two months, and the total loss was no less than tens of millions. However, Changsha only forced a donation of one or two million yuan, and a part of the public property was lost. This time, the Communist bandits attacked Changsha. All the public institutions, buildings, antiques, books, machinery, instruments, specimens, etc. in the whole city were burned, and the churches, schools, private houses were burned or demolished, the big merchants and wealthy households were looted or donated, and the deaths of people and the loss of family displacement were no less than 10,000,000. Changsha, the cultural, political, and commercial center of Hunan Province, which was known for its wealth, is now extremely desolate, and it is no longer as prosperous as it used to be. After the catastrophe, the remaining people are being comforted and gathered, but the suppression of bandits is in progress, and there is an urgent need for military expenses. Therefore, He Jian hired 25 leaders from the gentry and business circles, such as Zuo Xueqian, to form a Military Resources Committee to raise 2 million yuan in military expenses before the end of August. The decision was made to raise funds as follows: (1) Collect two months of rent from the provincial capital, about 200,000 yuan. (2) Each merchant will pay 300,000 yuan. (3) Borrow 500,000 yuan from each merchant with rice passports. (4) Send Shu Lijian to borrow 1,000,000 yuan from the Han business community, using rice passports or ore as collateral. As the number of funds is difficult to raise and the support is urgently needed, 200,000 yuan each from disaster relief funds and education funds were misappropriated to cope with it. The above belongs to the first batch of fundraising methods. As for the second batch of fundraising methods, it has been decided to hold a post-disaster donation to fill the needs of building fortresses, eliminating communist military needs, repairing government offices, developing social undertakings, and relief undertakings. The Military Resources Committee decided to collect eight articles of the post-disaster donation regulations and sent a letter to the provincial government and the four headquarters to comply with them. It is expected that the donation of more than 6,000,000 yuan can be collected within three months. The following is a record of the regulations, which shows the burden of the citizens of Changsha.

(Article 1) This committee will raise the following donations to raise the military expenses for eliminating the Communist Party and the post-disaster funds, but only once: (A) Tax on farmland rents and rents of lake land; (B) Tax on business capital; (C) Tax on houses in county towns and urban areas. (Article 2) The standards for the donation in the preceding article, except for the rent of lake land, which shall be subject to separate regulations, shall be collected in accordance with the progressive method as follows: (A) Tax on farmland rents: 1. From 200 stone to 500 stone of farmland rent, 4% shall be collected; 2. From 500 stone to 1,000 stone of farmland rent, 5% shall be collected; 3. From 1,000 stone to 1,500 stone of farmland rent, 6% shall be collected; 4. From 1,500 stone to 2,000 stone of farmland rent, 7% shall be collected; 5. From 2,000 stone to 3,000 stone of farmland rent, 10% shall be collected; 6. From 3,000 stone to 5,000 stone of farmland rent, 14% shall be collected; 7. For those with more than 5,000 stone of farmland rent, 16% shall be collected. (B) Tax on business capital: 1. For business capital between 5,000 yuan and 10,000 yuan, 1% shall be collected; 2. For business capital between 10,000 yuan and 20,000 yuan, 2% shall be collected; 3. For business capital between 20,000 yuan and 50,000 yuan, 3% shall be collected; 4. For business capital between 50,000 yuan and 100,000 yuan, 4% shall be collected; 5. For those with more than 100,000 yuan of business capital, 5% shall be collected. (C) Tax on houses in county towns and urban areas: 1. For houses in county towns and urban areas with a value of between 5,000 yuan and 10,000 yuan, 8‰ shall be collected; 2. For houses in county towns and urban areas with a value of between 10,000 yuan and 20,000 yuan, 9‰ shall be collected; 3. For houses in county towns and urban areas with a value of between 20,000 yuan and 30,000 yuan, 10‰ shall be collected; 4. For houses in county towns and urban areas with a value of between 30,000 yuan and 50,000 yuan, 11‰ shall be collected; 5. For houses in county towns and urban areas with a value of between 50,000 yuan and 100,000 yuan, 12‰ shall be collected; 6. For houses in county towns and urban areas with a value of between 100,000 yuan and 200,000 yuan, 13‰ shall be collected; 7. For those with more than 200,000 yuan of houses in county towns and urban areas, 14‰ shall be collected. (Article 3) The donations in the preceding article shall be handled by the county magistrate and the director of the finance bureau of each county by order of the provincial government, and the committee shall consider the situation and send personnel to supervise and manage the collection in different areas. The expenses of the collection and supervision personnel shall be determined separately. (Article 4) The collected donations shall be issued with three-part receipt, one part shall be handed over to the donor, one part shall be submitted to the committee, and the remaining part shall be kept in the county bureau for reference. (Article 5) If any donor conceals or evades the donation, once it is found or reported, they shall be punished separately according to the severity of the circumstances. (Article 6) If the personnel handling the matter solicit or embezzle the donation, they shall be dealt with by military law once the facts are verified. (Article 7) These regulations shall be sent to the provincial government for promulgation and implementation. (Article 8) If there are any unfulfilled matters in these regulations, they shall be resolved and revised by the committee.

Peng Dehuai Flees to Tonggu and Wanzai 59

Aircraft Conduct Daily Reconnaissance of Bandit Activity

Nanchang Dispatch: After Zhu De and Mao Zedong captured Shanggao and Yifeng, they engaged in widespread robbery and looting. The former Jiangxi Governor Hu Siyi's ancestral home in Yifeng, a very magnificent residence, has already been destroyed by the communist bandits. Other slightly well-known families have been completely ransacked. At present, the main force of the bandits is fleeing towards Wanzai, while smaller groups are scattering to Xinyu and Yichun counties, causing widespread disturbances. Peng Dehuai's bandit forces have retreated to Tonggu and Wanzai, and will temporarily remain in this area. Their future direction of escape and disruption seems undecided. Since the 14th, Lu Diping, in order to investigate bandit activity, has been dispatching a Moths No. 103 fighter plane daily to various locations for reconnaissance and bombing. The results of the past few days are as follows: (1) On the 14th, early in the morning, Tang Yuhe and Hu Zuqing piloted the Moths aircraft from Nanchang to the Gaoan, Shanggao, and Wanzai areas, distributing tens of thousands of leaflets. According to reports, communist bandits in Gaoan, Shanggao, and Wanzai were greatly panicked upon seeing the aircraft soaring in the sky and scattering leaflets, scattering and fleeing in all directions. (2) The border area between Yujiang and Xingui in eastern Jiangxi, 180 miles from the provincial capital, is a necessary route for the Rao River to reach the province. Since capturing Yiyang, Fang Zhimin's forces have invaded the county. On the morning of the 11th, the county seat and the Huangjinbu area were occupied by Fang's bandits. After receiving the report, Lu Diping, in addition to ordering the Zeng militia to suppress the bandits, specially ordered the Moths aircraft to conduct reconnaissance. On the morning of the 15th, Hu and Tang carried several heavy bombs and bundles of anti-bandit leaflets, flying to Yugan and Yujiang, returning to the province at 10 o'clock. According to their report, when flying to Yujiang, no traces of bandits were seen, but a group of communist bandits was discovered about twenty miles from the city. Two sixty-pound bombs were dropped on the bandit gathering, killing countless bandits, and the remaining bandits scattered. (3) On the morning of the 16th, the aircraft again flew to the Gaoan area for reconnaissance. Several hundred communist bandits were seen about ten miles from Gao City, fleeing in a disheveled manner. Several bombs were dropped, killing many bandits. Currently, the provincial party headquarters, in order to eliminate the communist bandits as soon as possible, has specially appointed Xiong Yuxi, Tian Keming, Yin Jingrang, and Wu Qisheng as four commissioners to go to Beijing and Hankou to petition for the rapid dispatch of a large army to Jiangxi. The four commissioners have set off today. The provincial government previously organized a guerrilla force from the security department, and has now also formally established the third police team and the armored train team of the Nanxun Railway. In the Ji'an area, because most of it has fallen into the bandit-controlled area, extremely strong defensive works, such as new-style trenches, gun emplacements, electric fences, and guard towers, are being gradually completed around the city. Twenty Communist Bandits Executed by Firing Squad in the Capital 60

Plotting to Launch an Uprising in the Capital in Support of the Hunan and Jiangxi Communist Bandits

The Capital Garrison Headquarters signed the order to execute twenty communist bandits by firing squad at Yuhuatai at 3 PM on the 18th. The process of arresting these communist bandits, the announcement of their crimes, and various other circumstances are recorded below.

Process of Arrest: Last month, the Investigation Department of the Capital Garrison Headquarters repeatedly received reports from secret agents that the Communist Party was plotting an uprising in the capital, hoping to respond to the communist bandits in Hunan and Jiangxi, and that many Communist Party members had been sent from Shanghai and Hankou to Beijing to participate in directing the operation. Based on these reports, the department immediately dispatched investigators to intensify the search and arrest. On the 29th of last month, an organization was uncovered on the upper floor of the Meihua Barber Shop in Xiaguan, and key criminals Guo Jintang, Wang Zhongbin, Li Xingguo, Li Yuanhe, Chen Yuhua, Song Ruhai, and others were arrested. A copy of the "Red Vanguard Team" organizational plan and a large package of various Communist Party leaflets, slogans, and printed materials were seized. On the same day, Li Chuankui, Jiang Zongluan, and Feng Bailiu were arrested on Shiba Street, and a large package of various Communist Party declarations, slogans, and printed materials were seized. Chen Jichang was arrested at Changsheng Temple, and several reactionary letters were seized. On August 5th, Fang Zhenlian, who was responsible for organizing rickshaw pullers' labor corps, was arrested in Binjiang Township, and several Communist Party printed materials were seized. On the 7th, a Communist Party printing center was uncovered in Yizhi Garden, and Tang Zao was arrested. An mimeograph machine, and two wax stencils with the draft of the declaration establishing the Second Division of the Fourteenth Army of the Chinese Red Army, were seized. Subsequently, based on Tang Zao's confession, Fu Linbo and Wang Housheng were arrested at Dashamao Lane, and an mimeograph machine and various reactionary printed materials were seized. On the same day, Huang Xiangbin, the secretary of the Communist Party branch of a certain school, was arrested in the school, and several letters between fellow party members were seized. On the 10th, the Communist Party's Nanjing Municipal Committee office was uncovered on Chengxian Street, and the pseudo-Municipal Committee member Ren Xuetao, and the pseudo-Northern District Committee member Tan Jianian were arrested. Several important announcements from the pseudo-Central and pseudo-Jiangsu Provincial Committees, and several recent work plans of the pseudo-Municipal Committee, and a list of contact names of their party members were seized. As a result, Lei Zhongyun and Shen Yishan, who were responsible for transmitting important news between Beijing and Shanghai for the party, were arrested at the Tailai Hotel, and Zhang Yimin, a party member sent to the Red Army to engage in military work, was arrested at the Jiangsu Hotel. All of the above criminals have been subjected to separate investigations by the military law department of the headquarters.

Page 12

The testimonies were deemed conclusive, and all were sentenced to death. In addition, there are several other cases and many suspects involved in those cases that have not yet been clearly investigated. These cases will not be announced for the time being. The twenty individuals sentenced to death, including Ren Xuetao, were brought in yesterday, the 18th, at 3 PM to verify their identities. Led by Adjutant Yuan Yangsheng, a team escorted the prisoners to Yuhuatai, outside of Zhonghua Gate to be executed by firing squad, in order to serve as a warning.

Circumstances at the Time of Execution: After the news of the Garrison Headquarters executing communist bandits by firing squad spread, the area in front of the department, including Dongpailou and the Confucius Temple, was crowded with onlookers from around 2 PM. At 3:15 PM, the criminals were brought out one by one. Military Judge Gu Bisheng used a red pen to mark their tags on the spot, verified their identities, had them drink alcohol and insert the tags, and then tied them into rickshaws. When the bandits were being tied up, they sang "The Internationale" and shouted reactionary slogans, appearing calm and unafraid. They were escorted by the Special Task Force of the headquarters, together with the cavalry of the Capital Police Department. Supervising Officer Yuan Yangsheng rode a horse alongside. Many people watched along the way. At the time of the execution, the bandits stretched their necks and waited, showing no signs of fear. In about fifteen minutes, these twenty Communist Party members returned to the underworld, one by one.

Announcement of Crimes: Regarding the announcement of the crimes, according to the head of the Investigation Department of the headquarters, Tian Jingxing, the following Communist Party members were arrested after uncovering Communist Party organizations in Beijing: Ren Yao, also known as Ren Xusheng (i.e., Ren Xuetao), Tan Jianian (alias Tao Bin, also known as Tao Yiyuan), Guo Jintang (i.e., Guo Hongxun, alias Zhongda), Li Xingguo, Li Weixuan (i.e., Li Gongfang, alias Wang Zhongbin, also alias Zhou Zhiqing), Huang Xiangbin, Song Ruhai, Tang Zao (alias Yang Zaiwen), Fu Linbo (alias Huang Longxian, also known as Chen Zhangjin), Wang Mengxian (alias Wang Housheng), Li Yuanhe, Chen Yuhua, Lei Zhongyun (i.e., Lei Yunong), Shen Yishan, Zhang Yimin (i.e., Zhang Zhengan), Chen Jichang (i.e., Chen Fanbo), Li Chuankui (i.e., Li Qiyu), Jiang Guangluan (i.e., Jiang Zhongyi), Feng Bailiu (i.e., Feng Chunhui), Fang Zhennian (i.e., Fang Zhenlian), and twenty other individuals. In addition, various Communist Party plans and propaganda materials were seized from the residences of these criminals. After separate interrogations by the headquarters, and mutual corroboration, it was confirmed that these twenty individuals, including Ren Yao and Guo Jintang, were indeed important members of the Communist Party. Some had been secretly active in Beijing, while others had come from Shanghai and Hankou to instigate conspiracies. According to the confessions of all the criminals, and various pieces of evidence, they had all been commissioned by the Third International, hoping to deceive the masses, exploit workers and peasants, incite soldiers, collude with bandits, disrupt public security in the capital, and respond to the communist uprisings in Hunan and Jiangxi. Their crimes were extremely heinous and unforgivable. It is ordered that Ren Yao, Tan Jianian, Guo Jintang, Li Xingguo, Li Weixuan, Huang Xiangbin, Song Ruhai, Tang Zao, Fu Linbo, Wang Mengxian, Li Yuanhe, Chen Yuhua, Lei Zhongyun, Shen Yishan, Zhang Yimin, Chen Jichang, Li Chuankui, Jiang Zongluan, Feng Bailiu, and Fang Zhennian be sentenced to death in order to serve as a warning. In addition to signing the order to bring in the criminals to verify their identities and tie them up for execution by firing squad, the crimes are hereby announced to inform the public. This proclamation.

Zhang Xueliang Goes to Beidaihe 61

Shenyang Dispatch: Zhang Xueliang, Commander of the Northeast Border Defense, is going to Beidaihe to escape the summer heat. This decision had been made before going to Huludao, but after arriving in Huludao, he felt slightly unwell. Because Beidaihe is inhabited by both Chinese and foreigners, and many representatives gather there, it is not conducive to quiet recuperation. In addition, the security in Huludao is tight, unlike the complexity of Beidaihe. Therefore, the temporary decision was canceled. Now that the weather is getting cooler, if it were not for the water obstructions in Beining, he would be returning to the provincial capital. A few days ago, he received an invitation from the commander of the British Navy, whose ships were entering the port in Qinhuangdao, and thus made another trip to Beidaihe. On the morning of the 11th, accompanied by National Government representatives Fang Benren and Zhang Qun and his wife, Ms. Yu Fengzhi, as well as other staff, he arrived in Beidaihe by car. On the afternoon of the 12th, he visited the British Navy warship. That evening, the British Navy commander hosted a banquet for Mr. and Mrs. Zhang. It is heard that Mr. Zhang plans to stay in Beidaihe for a short time before returning to the province to sort out various accumulated military and political affairs of the past month. Currently, Northeast representative Tang Erhe has gone to Beidaihe to meet with Zhang. (14th)

Extremely Severe Flooding in Liaoning 62

Shenyang Dispatch: Due to continuous heavy rain in Liaoning Province, rivers have overflowed, and countless people's homes, railway tracks, and bridges have been washed away and submerged. The authorities initially hoped to remedy the situation after the weather cleared up, but the weather is unpredictable. After every few days of sunshine, there is a rainstorm. As a result, traffic on all roads is blocked, with water depths reaching seven or eight feet, and transportation is completely interrupted. Repairs are repeatedly washed away. The provincial government has received disaster reports from various places, almost like snowflakes. The telegram from Suizhong County roughly states that in the county on the 3rd and 4th, waterfalls erupted in the mountains, tides rose in the sea, and rivers flooded without anywhere to go. The county seat and streets were completely washed away, with over 3,000 homes in the city and suburbs affected, and 2,000 men and women drowned or swept away. The affected area extends 400-500 li east-west and over 100 li north-south. The county has temporarily set up porridge kitchens to provide relief to the disaster-stricken people, but it is feared that its capacity cannot be extended for long, and its grain reserves are low, making it difficult to sustain. It requests to first draw upon accumulated grain reserves and funds to alleviate the immediate needs, and also requests that personnel be sent to inspect the situation and allocate 1,000 shi of relief grain and 400 tons of lump coal. In addition, more than 1,000 people were drowned in the area west of the Raoyang River over the course of the 12th and 13th. There are still refugees trapped by the water. After verification by the Liaoning Branch of the Red Swastika Society of the World in the provincial capital, it was decided that President Tan Tiehuang should visit Provincial Chairman Zang Shiyi and request that the Transportation Committee be informed by telegram to instruct the Beining Railway to allocate a locomotive, three covered freight cars, and one flatcar to facilitate the society's transport of disaster relief grain. The society purchased 5,000 jin of large flatbreads in the city and suburbs, and also purchased three large wooden boats, which were escorted by the organized temporary relief team to the Baiqibao area of the Raoyang River in Xinmin County for emergency use. It is heard that after arriving in Xinmin, another 1,000 dan of grain will be purchased and distributed. In addition, the river water has surged along the Beining Railway line, and the current is extremely turbulent. Obstructions have occurred successively between Xinmin and Liuhegou on the Ping-Shen main line, between Baiqibao and Raoyang River, between Raoyang River and Dahushan, and at the Nüer River in Jin County. Starting from the 4th of the month, round-trip trains have been suspended. Although the railway authorities are supervising workers to rush repairs, the rain comes again as soon as the repairs are completed, and they are washed away again. The situation in each section is mostly the same, and the resumption of traffic is still far off. The Yingkou and Datong branch lines have also been obstructed due to flooding. It is heard that the total loss of the railway is estimated at 1,560,000 yuan. (14th)

Railway Materials Still Allowed to be Tax-Exempt 63

Ministry of Railways Argues That There Should Be No Restrictions According to the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Contract. The Ministry of Railways previously reported that the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Bureau had stated that the Ministry of Finance had recently declared that the one-year tax exemption for materials of state-owned railways had expired and would not be extended. However, those railways with loan contract relationships should still be granted tax exemption in accordance with the contract provisions. The Ministry of Railways consulted with the Ministry of Finance to handle the matter. The Ministry of Finance replied that the 14th clause of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway loan contract in English only refers to the materials needed for construction, and does not mention materials for train operation and road maintenance. The so-called precedent of the Beiyang Railway should be limited to the materials needed for construction. Now that the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway has long been completed, it is difficult to grant further tax exemption. The Ministry of Railways believes that the 14th clause of the contract clearly states that all materials needed for the construction of the main line and branch lines, whether imported from overseas or transported from other provinces, are exempt from customs duties and likin, according to the precedent of the Beiyang Railway. The stipulation is very clear, and the original text contains the phrase "according to the precedent of the Beiyang Railway." This loan contract was signed in the 29th year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty. The so-called "precedent of the Beiyang Railway" at that time should refer to the contract of the Dongqing Railway Company in the 22nd year of Guangxu and the traffic contract of the Luhai Railway in the 24th year of Guangxu. Clause 7 of the Dongqing Railway Company contract states that all materials needed by the company for the construction and repair of the railway should be exempt from various taxes and likin. Clause 9 of the Luhai Railway traffic contract states that all materials needed by the company for train operation and road maintenance, when transported from foreign countries, should be exempt from customs duties and likin. According to the provisions of the above two contracts, all materials for construction, repair, train operation, and road maintenance are tax-exempt, with no time limit. The Shanghai-Nanjing Railway contract having declared its reliance on the precedent, it is not appropriate to impose restrictions. The Ministry of Railways has submitted the above reasons to the Executive Yuan for review, and requested that the Ministry of Finance be instructed to continue to handle the matter in accordance with the previous tax exemption methods. It is heard that after receiving the submission, the Executive Yuan has instructed that the original plan be maintained.

Local Dispatch

Songjiang 64

Details of the Shareholders' Meeting of the Huanan Agricultural Farm: The shareholders' meeting of the Huanan Agricultural Farm in Xinzhuang Town, western Shanghai, was held at the farm at 1 PM on August 17th. More than ten shareholders, including Li Qixian and Tang Dixian, attended the meeting as scheduled. Mr. Wu Shudu first reported on the progress of the farm's affairs and its business situation. All shareholders deemed the management to be proper and unanimously approved it. The meeting continued to discuss proposals, such as the method of paying official interest, future development direction, and plans for improving and expanding equipment. Appropriate methods were agreed upon for all proposals. It is heard that the farm is quite developed and is currently actively expanding.

The Crime of Extortion by Bandits: Cai Yisheng, a villager in Xihutang Township, Punan, cultivates dozens of acres of farmland. He is diligent and thrifty, and his family can barely make a living. At the beginning of last month, three bandits carrying box-shaped pistols sent a letter demanding 1,000 yuan, to be collected by the 20th. At the same time, Xu Maoxiang, who lived nearby, also received a letter demanding 800 yuan. Xu was timid by nature, and became anxious and ill after receiving the letter, leading to his death. When the due date arrived for Cai Yisheng, three bandits came, around 9 PM. The villagers had already gone to bed. The bandits deceived Cai Yisheng by claiming they needed to borrow a boat, and then seized him and demanded the money. Cai, intimidated by the bandits, immediately scraped together 200 yuan from neighbors. The bandits seemed unsatisfied, but Cai could not raise any more money. They set a deadline of three days for their return and asked Cai to meet them at Nanyang Lou in Shanyang Town for tea. However, the bandits' route of departure was along a small path leading to Shanyang, indicating that an acquaintance must have been involved. The bandits also spoke in a local dialect, providing clues that the authorities should be able to use to apprehend them.

Petition to Relieve Prison Overcrowding: The county prison has three large cells and eight small cells, which can accommodate about 100 people. Recently, due to the increase in criminals, the prison is housing over 180 inmates, and there are also those detained pending trial, not included in that number. As the weather is hot, the cramped conditions can easily lead to disease. To alleviate the overcrowding, Warden Zhang plans to transfer 40 inmates to other prisons. In addition, there are 20 inmates from Shanghai No. 2 Prison being held there. After six are released upon completion of their sentences, there will be 14 remaining, and he has requested that the Shanghai prison take them back. It is heard that a roster has been prepared and submitted to the county government for forwarding to the High Court for approval.

Suzhou 65

Garrison Headquarters Comes to Suzhou to Escort Key Criminals: The Capital Garrison Headquarters yesterday instructed four soldiers, including Ma Chongxing, to come to Suzhou with official documents to escort two key anti-revolutionary criminals, Li Yuzhe and Ju Shilin, from the High Court. They were taken from the Third Detention Center in the morning and escorted back to Nanjing for further investigation.

Newly Appointed Prison Warden of Fengxian Resigns: In the case of the escape of 58 prisoners from Fengxian County Prison, Chief Judge Lin of the High Court ordered Warden Liu Ou to be investigated by the Shanghai District Court. Miao Wengui was appointed to fill the vacancy. After being appointed, Miao went to Fengxian to investigate the incident. He believed that the prisoners' escape was caused by the incitement of reactionary elements, and not due to Warden Liu's negligence. Therefore, he came to Suzhou yesterday to meet with Chief Judge Lin, explained the situation in detail, and requested that Warden Liu not be held responsible. As for himself, he resigned from the position of prison warden of the county on the spot.

Impersonating a Soldier for Extortion Leads to Arrest and Execution by Firing Squad: The Fourth Regiment of the Suzhou Garrison reported on the 18th that Xu Jinbao, a boatman, reported that Xia Dahua, a native of Dongtai, was wearing a uniform and impersonating a soldier to extort money in the area outside Chanxu Gate. Commander Xuan immediately sent troops to arrest Xia in a small teahouse on the road. As a result of the interrogation with Xu, Xia Dahua confessed that he was 25 years old and admitted to extorting money from the boatman Xu Jinbao and impersonating the regiment. Therefore, at 10:30 AM yesterday, the 19th, the criminal was tied up and executed by firing squad on Liuyuan Road, and his crimes were announced as a warning.

The Details of the Communist Bandit Prison Break in Qidong: Regarding the case of the communist bandits breaking into the Qidong County detention center and setting it on fire on the evening of the 8th of this month, Judicial Commissioner Zhu Zhongqi, appointed by Chief Judge Lin of the High Court, went to investigate the incident in detail on the 14th of this month and reported back to Suzhou yesterday. According to the investigation conducted by Commissioner Zhu this time, the circumstances are as follows: Previously, the county had captured the communist bandit leader Zhao Keming and detained him in the detention center. County Magistrate Xia Yueqing reported the matter to the province, ordering that he be sent to the Songhu Garrison Commander for investigation. The communist bandit comrades learned of the matter and, on the evening of the 8th, gathered more than 300 people, armed with rifles, wooden sticks, broadswords, etc., broke into the detention center from behind by destroying the wall, releasing more than 60 prisoners. More than 30 people were still inside when the bandits set the building on fire. Fortunately, a pirate who had not escaped did his best to extinguish the flames. Subsequently, 50 police officers from the county went to pursue the bandits, who had fled and scattered into the cotton fields in the countryside. The police officers, fearing that they would be surrounded by the bandits, returned to the county to maintain order. After receiving the report, Chief Judge Lin, noting that the fire was extinguished by pirates, ordered the county to be given a lighter punishment.

Lawyer Sues County Magistrate, Investigation to be Sent: Lawyer Zhang Qingyue recently filed a lawsuit with the High Court accusing Liang Zihou, the magistrate of Chongming County, of corruption and harming the people, among other charges. Yesterday, the High Court instructed the chief prosecutor of the Shanghai District Court to send personnel to investigate the allegations clearly before making a decision.

Fengxian 66

Request to Postpone County Collection of Salt Field Taxes: The elders of the county, Tao Wangkan and others, believe that the county government's plan to collect salt field taxes at the county level in order to combine them with the busy season tax is not in line with local conditions. Therefore, they requested a postponement the day before yesterday. Their reasons are: (1) Salt fields outside the sea dike are called "Dangdi," and the soil is salty and barren, yielding little. Salt fields inside the dike also have shallow ditches, and there is a saying that they yield three harvests every nine years. Therefore, past authorities have always taxed them lightly. (2) Both the inner and outer salt fields are low-lying and require dredging ditches and adding mud every year. During high tides, the reeds and fields are still prone to being washed away. Therefore, these fields cannot be compared to the cultivated land in the county. Now, the county government claims that combining the busy season tax with salt field taxes will increase revenue by 100,000 yuan per year, causing the people to spread the news in alarm and feel insecure. Although this case concerns changes in the administrative system between the county and its field, there will be a decision by the superiors. The people are all paying taxes, so there is no need to dwell on it. However, the principle of increasing taxes should be based on whether they can be borne and should be implemented gradually. It should not be rushed. The people would be grateful if the county could refrain from persisting in its opinion.

Southern Fengxian Joint Defense Approved by Provincial Order: Ding Zhiyan, captain of the county police brigade, previously stated that the border area in southern Fengxian is easily used to hide bandits, making arrest and pursuit difficult. Therefore, he consulted with Zhang Yiyi, the fifth district chief of the county, and obtained his agreement. Now, the Nanhui County sent a letter stating that the fifth district had reported Captain Ding's proposal for joint defense in southern Fengxian. The proposal has been approved by the provincial government. Therefore, County Magistrate Shen has now drafted a joint defense plan for reporting at a meeting. He will also initiate a joint defense conference involving the five counties of Songjiang, Fengxian, Jinshan, Nanhui, and Shanghai to thoroughly eliminate bandits.

The New Heads of the Chambers of Commerce in Nanqiao and Zhuangxing are Declared After Mutual Selection: Regarding the re-election of the chambers of commerce in Zhuangxing and Nanqiao, it is known that the two chambers held mutual elections the day before yesterday. In Zhuangxing, Shen Qiucha was elected chairman, and Gu Renan and Fan Jiyan were elected standing members. In Nanqiao, Wu Hongxiang was elected chairman, and Li Tianmin and Xiao Jincai were elected standing members. They are scheduled to be sworn in next week.

Wuxi 67

They requested that officials be dispatched quickly to investigate thoroughly to deter corruption.

A Rural Woman in Huacheng Lane Gives Birth to a Monstrous Fetus: In Huacheng Lane, located about three miles from Zhangjingqiao Town in the seventh district of Xiyi (Huai Shang City), there lives a farmer named Chen Yaogen, who is engaged in agriculture and has a modest family fortune. His wife, Zhou, who is 37 years old, became pregnant last winter and carried the pregnancy to term. Yesterday afternoon around 4 p.m., Zhou suddenly felt abdominal pain and knew she was about to give birth. She quickly summoned a midwife to attend to her at home. Shortly after, she gave birth to a monstrous fetus. The child had a white fleshy horn on its head, about three inches long, and its head resembled that of an animal, but its hands and feet were the same as those of a normal child. Mr. and Mrs. Chen were very surprised to see this monstrous child and considered it ominous, planning to abandon it in the wilderness. Those who came to see it were amazed, but the monstrous fetus died about an hour after birth.

Three Bandits from Wujin Recant in Court: Xue Furi, captain of the detective team of the local Public Security Bureau, captured three major suspects in the Wujin kidnapping case, Jiang Jigen, Gong Ahui, and Zhu Jinsheng, at the Railway Hotel the night before last. Two unmailed letters were also found. During the interrogation, Jiang Jigen confessed to one robbery, stating that he and Zhang Agen, a farmer from Outangqiao, and Zhu Jinsheng came to Wuxi to commit a robbery near Meiyuan, which failed, leading to their arrest. Gong Ahui confessed to two robberies, and Zhu Jinsheng confessed to four robberies and kidnappings. It is rumored that the robbery of the Zhou Tieqiao to Wuxi boat was also committed by the above three criminals. Yesterday afternoon, Captain Xue prepared a document and sent them to the bureau. Section member Bao Tiyu of the Third Section opened the court for interrogation. However, Jiang Jigen and the other two suddenly recanted their confessions. After three hours of interrogation, no conclusive confession was obtained. After the interrogation, they were sent to the county government for trial. It is reported that the Wujin County Government will send personnel to Wuxi within a few days to escort them back for trial.

Subsidizing the Long-Distance Telephone Expenses of Nine Counties: The long-distance telephone lines of nine counties in Jiangsu Province are now planned to be expanded, passing through Wujin directly to Suzhou. The Provincial Long-Distance Telephone Administration has made detailed plans. Four-tenths of the entire line project has been completed, but the total project cost is still short of 15,000 yuan. A special request has been submitted to the Construction Department to have the costs shared by the three counties of Wuxi, Xiyi, and Suzhou, and to allocate funds from the original construction funds of each county for advance payment. Once the Financial Department allocates the project funds for the line, the advance payments will be reimbursed. The amount to be shared is determined based on the length of the line: Wuxi 6,000 yuan, Xiyi 6,000 yuan, Suzhou 5,000 yuan, and Wujin 4,000 yuan. The Wuxi County Construction Bureau has been ordered to allocate 6,000 yuan from the collected construction funds and report it to the Construction Department for use.

Changzhou 68

An Arson Case Due to Grudges in the Sixth District: Wang Kuide of Chenghe Township in the sixth district of Wujin County is the uncle of Li Renbao. Li Renbao had long coveted Wang Kuide's widowed daughter-in-law, who was approaching thirty. Wang Kuide refused, leading to a feud. A few days ago, Li prepared five boxes of matches and went to Wang's house to set fire, which spread to more than ten houses. Li was soon arrested and reported by the district office to the court for trial on the 18th. Li confessed to setting the fire and burning the houses. The court ordered him to be shackled and imprisoned, and scheduled a summons for Wang Kuide to be brought to court for questioning on the 21st.

Jiangyin 69

Qiaoqi Villagers Arrest Chen Wei Wu: The Rizhao area of Qiaoqi Township is adjacent to Qin Nan Yue Dong. There are many villages, divided into the second and eighteenth districts. Since the beginning of summer, Gao Caifu of the Zhulin Nunnery in that area, due to his association with the Communist Party, gathered with accomplices from Nanwai Gaosong Bridge and other places. The villagers resented this. On the night of the 16th, they surrounded the Zhulin Nunnery and captured Wang Guozhen and Gao Caibao, along with one handgun, seven bullets, a list of party members, and a list of planned work locations. On the morning of the 18th, the district defense corps handed them over to the county government. In the afternoon, County Magistrate Li secretly interrogated them. According to Wang Guozhen's confession, his real name is Chen Wei Wu, alias Wang Guozhen, 28 years old, residing in Xiheng Street in the city. His father's name is Ji Xi. He joined the Communist Party after the Nationalist Party went public and has been away for two years. He returned to Cheng a week ago, ordered by the higher party department to correct the mistakes in Jiangyin's party affairs. He also spoke extensively about his doctrines. Gao Caibao confessed that Chen Wei Wu came to the township to work with his cousin Caifu, and the handgun was found on Chen's person. After the interrogation, they were taken into custody. In the evening, the Director of Public Security conducted another interrogation.

Zhenjiang 70

Security Department Prevents Banditry in Jiangbei: The Jiangsu Provincial Security Department telegraphed the county magistrates of Jiangbei Nantong Xinghua and other counties yesterday, stating that reliable reports indicate that rebel Ma Yuren is currently gathering bandits, local thugs, and communists to invade Yancheng and Fu, taking advantage of the situation to riot. In order to eliminate banditry and consolidate the rear, this department has stipulated that the first, third, and third brigade commander Liu Hanzhen be responsible for the suppression of banditry in Xinghua, Yancheng, Funing, Huai'an, Gaoyou, Baoying, Huaiyin, and Siyang counties. The third regiment commander Li Changjiang is responsible for the suppression of banditry in Jingjiang, Dongtai, Jiangyin, Taixing, Nantong, Taixian, Qidong, and Haimen counties. They are also ordered to communicate with each other and respond to situations at any time.

Endless Banditry Cases: More than ten bandits, armed with box cannons, suddenly came to Hanjia Village in Yucheng Township, Zhenjiang, at the second watch last night, rushed into the house and kidnapped Zeng Bangquan's son, Chenggan (11 years old), leaving a note demanding 5,000 yuan, agreeing to negotiate at Jingxian Mountain on the afternoon of the third day. Also, in Huang Village in the west township, about twenty or thirty bandits suddenly came at about 5 p.m. yesterday, surrounded the village, and fired guns to show their power. The joint defense corps of the village joined forces to encircle and capture them. The bandits resisted by firing guns. After ten minutes of stalemate, they knew they were no match and fled to the Changshan area. Most disgustingly, the bandits set fire to the Xia family's house before leaving.

Agricultural Department Dispatches Agricultural Surveyors: The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture believes that the agricultural surveys for the 18th year have been completed separately, and all agricultural surveys for the 19th year should begin immediately. Huzhou 75

The Entire Town of Hengshan Bridge Robbed by Bandits: Hengshan Bridge Town in the northern countryside of Changxing County, Huzhou, has more than twenty shops. Although it is a small place, its commerce is very developed. At about 1 p.m. on the 15th, seven or eight bandit ships suddenly arrived and stopped outside the town. More than fifty bandits, speaking with mixed accents, each holding guns, guarded the two ends of the town, and the remaining bandits broke into the town and robbed it. More than twenty shops, large and small, were spared. The looting lasted for an hour, and then the bandits fired guns to show their power and fled. The exact amount of the losses is not yet known, but the butcher shop and a certain rice shop suffered the greatest losses. It was also heard that a 17-year-old girl from a certain family was kidnapped by the bandits before they left. It is also said that a wealthy gentleman named Chen was kidnapped, but whether this is true remains to be verified.

Another Child Kidnapped in Taiziwan: Shi Guangnian's grandson in Taizihai in the northwestern countryside of the city was kidnapped by bandits at 6 p.m. on the 15th of this month, leaving a letter demanding a large ransom. Unexpectedly, at about 5 p.m. the next day, three bandits with wooden shell guns suddenly broke into the village, first firing guns to show their power. At that time, Shi Liankui's son, only five years old, was playing outside his house and was taken away by the bandits.

Local News

Liu Yunfang Re-visits French Consul Yesterday 78

Regarding the Jinliyuan Wharf Case

Inquiring About the Reasons for the French Court's Continued Hearing

Approaching Steps for Arbitration

Regarding the dispute over the Jinliyuan Wharf of the China Merchants Bureau, the results of the negotiations between Cai Ziping, Acting General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau, and Liu Yunfang, Director of the Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and French Consul General Gager, to prevent the French court from executing the ruling and to proceed with arbitration immediately, were recorded in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that yesterday afternoon at 2:00 p.m., Mr. Teipke, the lawyer representing the China Merchants Bureau, suddenly reported to General Manager Cai by telephone that he had received a notice from the French Court of Public Affairs that the case would be re-heard at 3:00 p.m. today (i.e., yesterday) and requested that Teipke appear in court as a representative. General Manager Cai replied that the French Consul had already clearly expressed the day before that the execution of the Public Affairs Office would be prevented. Why was it still necessary to re-hear the case? While asking lawyer Teipke to appear in court as a representative to declare the remarks made by the French Consul the day before, he also invited Director Liu Yunfang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to visit the French Consul General again to inquire about the matter. Mr. Liu went to the French Consulate at 3:30 p.m. to meet with Consul General Gan and stated that since the case had been discussed the day before and arbitration procedures were underway, the legal proceedings should be stopped immediately. Why did the French Court of Public Affairs still re-hear the case at 3:00 p.m. today? Moreover, your Consul General has clearly stated and guaranteed to prevent execution. What is the purpose of the re-hearing today? Consul General Gan replied that the hearing today was because the previous date was scheduled as the date of review, and it must be done procedurally. Your representative lawyer can appear in court as usual. Although the Consul General is not a judge, he can be responsible for ensuring that the result of the re-hearing today will still not result in execution. Mr. Liu considered the reply satisfactory and then discussed the steps for arbitration. Mr. Liu said that the arbitrator of the China Merchants Bureau had been designated by General Manager Cai the day before. Your Consul General should notify the priest as soon as possible to start the negotiations between the arbitrators as soon as possible. According to the French Consul, he hoped that the China Merchants Bureau would prepare a plan for guaranteeing future rent payments on time as soon as possible. If the rent is to be paid by a bank, this document should be submitted to the French Consul General for study first, and then the French Consul General should persuade the priest of the San De Church to accept the plan. Then the arbitrator of the San De Church will formally discuss the lease issue with the arbitrator of the China Merchants Bureau. It is okay to continue to maintain the old agreement, and it is also okay for both parties to sign a new agreement. Even if a new agreement is signed, its content will not be much different from the old agreement. Consul General French finally stated to Director Liu that the water and electricity storm in the French Concession and the Jinliyuan Wharf case were all local events and not political cases. It is gratifying that the authorities and people of the two countries have resolved them peacefully with a spirit of mutual understanding. Director Liu also considered the French Consul's remarks to be satisfactory and shook hands and parted ways. He also conveyed the content of the French Consul's remarks to General Manager Cai. General Manager Cai expressed satisfaction and planned to proceed with the arbitration immediately based on the results of the talks.

Contents of Sino-German Aviation Contract 81

Total Capital of Three Million

Chinese Shares Account for Two-Thirds

The Sino-German Aviation Contract was signed by Minister of Communications Wang Boqun and Schmidt, the representative of the German Aviation Company, in Beijing on February 21 of this year. On the 13th of this month, Minister Wang Schmidt held another meeting in Beijing, waiting for the approval of both parties before it can take effect. The contents of the contract learned by the Xinzheng News Agency are as follows:

Total Capital: The total capital of the company is 3 million yuan in national currency, divided into 3,000 shares. China will recognize 2,000 shares and Germany will recognize 1,000 shares. Both parties will pay within three months. China will pay 200,000 and Germany will pay 100,000. Within nine months, Germany will advance funds to purchase machinery and supplies and issue stocks according to the amount of the advance.

Company Organization: The company will have a board of directors with nine directors elected according to the number of shares. There will be one chairman and two vice-chairmen. One of the vice-chairmen will be appointed by Germany. The board of directors will have three groups: operations, finance, and aviation. The director of aviation and the deputy director of finance will be appointed by Germany. The income will be deposited in the Bank of China.

Route Distribution: (1) From Shanghai via Nanjing, Tianjin, Beijing, Manchuria, and Siberia to Europe. (2) From Shanghai via Nanjing, Tianjin, Beijing, Kulun, and Siberia to Europe. (3) From Shanghai via Nanjing, Xinjiang, Gansu, and Siberia to Europe.
