Pharmaceutical Industry Workers' Union Submits Document to Municipal Party Headquarters

Requesting Correction of Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's Criticisms

The Shanghai Pharmaceutical Industry Workers' Union submitted a document to the Municipal... Yun, requesting that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has not clarified the truth about the addition of a representative from Tongkang Pharmacy and has made unwarranted criticisms. Since the Central Government promulgated the Law on Industrial and Commercial Associations, the union has never violated explicit orders or forced members not to join the association. However, after Tongkang Pharmacy added employee Zhang Qinzhang as a representative to the association, the union repeatedly and cautiously investigated, in accordance with the law, whether the average number of employees used by Tongkang Pharmacy in the past year exceeded fifteen. According to the investigation results, the number of employees used by the pharmacy still does not meet the regulations of the law. Therefore, the addition of an employee representative is naturally unnecessary. This is the first point that the union must legally fight for. Recently, on July 17, it was reported that the Central Political Conference dealt with the restriction on the qualifications of members' representatives in industrial and commercial associations. As a result of the research by Committee Member Dai Chuanxian and Committee Member Kong Xiangxi, it was recognized that the principle that employees should be allowed to serve as representatives of the association should be respected. However, the premise of the association to promote the common interests of the industry and correct business malpractices should also be taken into account. It is essential that labour and management coordinate, and that the two parties help and understand each other in order to achieve effective cooperation. Therefore, Article 7 of the law, which concerns the qualification of member representatives, has been revised to allow each company or firm to send one or two representatives, limited to managers or principals, but if the average number of employees in the most recent year is fifteen or more, one additional representative may be sent, who shall be mutually elected by the employees of each company or firm. This revised article has been adopted by the Central Political Conference. Looking at the above, the procedure for adding employee representatives requires that the employees of each company or firm mutually elect them. The addition of employee Zhang Qinzhang as a representative by Tongkang Pharmacy did not comply with the Central Government's revised laws and regulations, but was entrusted by Manager Du Maiqing in his personal capacity, which is illegal and exceeds his authority. This is the second point that the union must legally fight for. The Central Political Conference is the highest authority in the country for implementing policies. After any law is passed, the people of the country should absolutely abide by it. How could the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the highest organization leading the city's business community, not recognize the articles passed by the Central Political Conference and say that the union is abusing the law? This is too far from the truth and is intentionally disrespecting the Central Government. Furthermore, they say that the union is interfering and forcing Manager Du Xianqing of Tongkang Pharmacy, etc. The Chamber of Commerce does not seek the truth and makes unwarranted criticisms. This is extremely absurd. It is earnestly hoped that your committee will quickly correct this and reprimand them. In addition, it is requested that your committee immediately revoke the qualifications of employee Zhang Qinzhang as a representative from Tongkang Pharmacy. This would be of great benefit to the public.

Nihua Cotton Mill Labor Dispute Reported Yesterday

Management Announces Factory Closure for the Second Time

Labor Decides to Persist to the End

The management of Nihua Cotton Mill in Pudong, whose plot to entice striking workers back to work unconditionally was seen through by the workers and failed to succeed, suddenly announced the closure of the factory yesterday. However, the labor side regarded this as nothing and remained calm as usual. The details are as follows:

Factory Issues Closure Notice

After Nihua Cotton Mill issued a notice of resumption of work the day before yesterday and no one entered the factory, the factory was greatly angered. It changed its plan and adopted intimidating measures, suddenly posting a notice last night declaring the closure of the factory, hoping to soften the workers' persistent attitude.

Workers Not Moved in the Slightest

The workers, deeply aware that this kind of intimidation is a trick used by the Japanese, have declared the closure and opening of the factory twice since the strike began. Therefore, they regard this matter as a farce and remain unusually calm. They stated that even if the factory really closes, the workers will definitely not starve to death.

Union Expresses Attitude

The organizing committee of the factory's union believes that the Japanese's declaration of the closure of the factory this time is entirely an act of intimidation and can be ignored. If the factory really closes, then China's Jisheng Cotton Mill can take the opportunity to open a factory. China has one more domestic goods manufacturer, and workers can still find work.

Fundraising to Help Workers

The organizing committee of the factory's union believes that this strike must persist to the end. However, according to investigations, the workers' livelihood can be maintained for about three and a half months. However, it cannot be said for certain whether the Japanese will come to their senses after three and a half months. Therefore, they gathered last night to discuss and submitted a request to the Municipal Party Department to allow fundraising to provide relief. Once approved, they will start to proceed.

Pudong Labor Circles Donate First

According to recent news from various labor unions in Pudong, the demands of the Nihua workers have a great impact on various labor unions in Pudong. Because they have a personal connection, they must help them. Within two or three days, they will automatically convene a general meeting of representatives from various labor unions in Pudong to discuss how to deal with the Nihua Cotton Mill and use economic assistance to help the factory's workers. Then, they will send a letter to all labor unions in Shanghai, citing the method of aiding French business strikes, with each person donating one dollar.

French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association Sends Letter to Director-General Fei

Expressing Gratitude for Mediating Water and Electricity Labor Dispute

The water and electricity labor dispute in the French Concession has been resolved. The Chinese Taxpaying Association of the French Concession sent a letter to Director-General Fei of the French Municipal Council, expressing its gratitude. The letter reads, "Director-General Fei, respectfully informing you that the water and electricity workers' strike lasted for fifty-four days. Fortunately, Director-General Fei, in consultation with the Consul-General, managed the situation effectively, avoiding the spread of the issue and affecting public security. The citizens within the concession are truly grateful. After this resumption of work, it is hoped that your Director-General will instruct the tram company's superintendent to find ways to mediate between labor and management in the future, so that each party can be treated fairly. This will prevent any misunderstandings, stabilize local public security, and allow all businesses to flourish. Sincerely, we respectfully wish you well. Sincerely, the Chinese Taxpaying Association of the French Concession."

Relief and Comfort Association Holds Meeting Yesterday

Since the preparation for the Relief and Comfort Association for Disaster Victims in War Zones and Comforting Soldiers on the Front Lines began, it has been actively underway. Recently, donations from all sectors have been quite enthusiastic. The association held a joint meeting of various groups at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 3:00 PM yesterday to discuss the progress. Those present included Wang Yansong, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Hongjun, Zheng Huizhu, and over ten other people. The results are as follows: (1) Payments will be signed by Ye Huijun and Wang Xiaolai with the official seal. (2) Letters will be sent to those who have not yet made payments to urge them to do so. (3) Another meeting will be scheduled next week to discuss the situation.

Municipal Works Bureau to Repair Chaodong Dam in Gaohang District

There is a Chaodong Dam near Qingning Bridge at the western end of Yangjia Alley in the Gaohang District of the city. It was suddenly washed away by a storm a few days ago, and traffic was immediately cut off. Hundreds of acres of farmland nearby were flooded. The Municipal Port Affairs Bureau sent a letter to the Municipal Works Bureau, requesting that workers be sent to rebuild it immediately to facilitate wealth and protect the people's food supply. After receiving the letter, the Municipal Works Bureau immediately sent personnel to investigate, stating that the Chaodong Dam is closely related to water conservancy and transportation. The need to restore it quickly after it was washed away by the storm is necessary. A special report was submitted to the Municipal Government, requesting that funds be allocated for repairs. It was learned yesterday that the Municipal Government has issued an order approving the allocation.

Seventeen New Stations to be Added to Two Railways

Liu Weichi Granted Approval by the Ministry of Railways to Proceed as Planned

Liu Weichi, the director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Bureaus, proposed several measures to improve the two railways. Yesterday, the Ministry of Railways issued an order approving the proposals. Among them, the addition of new stations to the two railways is particularly aimed at facilitating passengers and will begin immediately in sequence. The original plan for the location of the new stations is as follows: (A) Twelve stations to be set up on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway: (1) Between Anting and Lujiabang, (2) Between Kunshan and Zhengyi, (3) Between Suzhou and Hushu Pass, (4) Between Wangting and Jinggang, (5) Between Wuxi and Shitangwan, (6) Between Luoshe, (7) Between Qishuyan and Changzhou, (8) Between Lucheng and Lingkou, (9) Between Xinfeng and Zhaze, (10) Between Zhenjiang and Gaozi, (11) Between Gaozi and Xiashu, (12) Between Xiashu and Longtan. (B) Five stations to be set up on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway: (1) Between Shihudang and Fengjing, (2) Between Jiashan and Jiaxing, (3) Between Jiaxing and Wangdian, (4) Between Xiashi and Xieqiao, (5) Between Linping and Jianqiao. The above plan will be implemented in order of urgency. The station between Anting and Lujiabang has already been put out to tender. In addition, it is said that the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway will first build the station between Shihudang and Fengjing, approximately one station per month. At the beginning of construction, maximum savings will be sought. Express trains will not stop at these stations. Ordinary express trains will be reconsidered. Generally, only slow trains going in both directions will stop at these stations.

Registered Letters to Nanyang Insurance

Must be Written in Roman Script

The Shanghai Postal Administration announced that when sending insured and registered letters to the Nanyang Islands and the Malay Federation, if only Chinese characters are used for names and addresses, it is quite inconvenient for delivery, and misdelivery is unavoidable. Therefore, all senders are notified to quickly obtain translated slips of the names and addresses of their relatives and friends in advance and affix them to the envelope for mailing. From now on, registered and insured letters sent to the destination must be written in Roman script so that the post office can accept them.

Important News from the Yangtze River Shipping Industry

Sanbei Increases Number of Newly Built Ships

In order to develop the shipping industry on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, the Sanbei Steamship Company will build two new Yangtze River steamers of less than 600 tons in this city, named Hongzeng and Hongli. Together with the already operational Hongyuan and Hongheng, they will form four sister ships for expanding the Yichang and Changsha routes on the upper Yangtze River. It is reported that both ships are under construction, and the hull of the ship will be completed in about two months.

Yichang Comes to Shanghai for Repair

The American-owned upstream steamer Yichang, of the Jejiang Company, was damaged in Wanxian while en route from Shanghai to Chongqing. It was immediately towed to Shanghai and is now being repaired at Ruirong Foundry. Yesterday, after inspection by the shipyard, it was determined that the machinery needed to be dismantled and a water-draining machine added before it could sail on the Yangtze River. It is currently under repair.

Sharp Decline in Passengers and Goods in Hankou

The authorities in Hankou recently issued a curfew order, cutting off traffic at 8:00 PM every day. Therefore, the cargo volume of downstream steamers from Hankou to Shanghai has drastically decreased. Because the various ports cannot work at night, the number of passengers traveling from Hankou to Shanghai has also greatly decreased, at least one-third compared to a week ago. Currently, there are a total of twenty-two warships from five countries, Britain, Japan, the United States, France, and Italy, docked in Hankou, reportedly the largest number of foreign ships berthed in Hankou.

Reply to Telegram Requesting Suppression of Communist Bandits in Northern Jiangsu

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the Fresh Pork Industry Association stating that the Communist bandits in northern Jiangsu were causing disturbances, making the transportation of fresh pork difficult, and requested the dispatch of troops to station and defend the area. After sending a telegram to the Jiangsu Provincial Government to request suppression, it has now received a telegram from the Jiangsu Provincial Government stating, "Telegram from Qing has been received. The Department of Civil Affairs and the Security Office have been ordered to jointly handle the matter."

The Famine Relief Society Solicits Aid for Victims in Xuchang and Mi County

Zhou Xiwun, a representative stationed in Shanghai of the Henan Province Famine Relief Society, recently received two telegrams from the province, which are transcribed below: (1) "To Shanghai, Beijing, and various charitable organizations and newspapers: According to reports from various agencies in Xuchang County, the county was heavily garrisoned by troops last winter, and the people are in extreme hardship. This spring, tens of thousands of troops are stationed, apportioning cash and providing grain, amounting to several million yuan. The people are impoverished and have exhausted their grain. They were hoping for a good wheat harvest in the autumn, but unexpectedly, war broke out again, and the entire county was reduced to a war zone. Dozens of days of fierce fighting resulted in wheat being abandoned on the ground, houses turned into ruins, corpses littering the fields, and chickens and dogs silenced. The southern part of the county also suffered hail, breaking off all the wheat ears, leaving no grain to harvest. It is extremely tragic and painful. Please provide urgent relief. Li Shizan, Chairman of the Henan Province Famine Relief Society." (2) "Abbreviated title: Recently, according to reports from various agencies in Mi County, the remaining people after the disaster have suffered repeated calamities. On May 4th, hail suddenly fell, with hailstones as large as bowls, lasting for about an hour. The wheat in areas such as Yuetai was completely destroyed, and many houses and livestock were damaged. In areas with less severe damage, the wheat harvest was reduced by 60-70%. In the northeastern area of Guanyintang, when the wheat was being threshed, more than a thousand bandits suddenly came, attacking, killing, burning, and looting, burning all the stacked wheat in the fields in the area. The hope of a wheat harvest has been dashed. On June 15th, hail fell again, as large as fists, lasting for about fifty minutes, accumulating to a thickness of about five inches, causing the fields in the northeastern and southeastern areas to be completely destroyed. The central area is suffering from extreme drought, with the seedlings withered, and the autumn harvest is hopeless again. The sound of crying fills the roads, begging for urgent relief. It is reported that the remaining people in the county are waiting to be saved, but natural and man-made disasters continue to increase. Remaining lives are hanging by a thread. It is hoped that kind-hearted people from all walks of life will show great compassion and provide large-scale relief to save the people. Li Shizan, Chairman of the Henan Province Famine Relief Society." It is reported that Representative Zhou, after receiving these two telegrams, went to various charitable organizations to plead for relief.

The Resignation of the Fifth District Chief of the County Approved

Peng Liren, the chief of the Fifth District of Shanghai County, submitted his resignation, which has been approved by the County Government. Establishment of the Book Industry Tongle Association

The Book Industry Tongle Association, initiated by Wang Songliang, assistant manager of Saoyeshanfang Bookstore, was established in Duyichu the night before last. The members included Wang Jinnan and Zhang Ziqian from World Bookstore, Xu Heling from Baixin Company, Yin Zhongqing from Hongbaozhai, Gao Wenhe from Cuiying Bookstore, Zhou Chucai from Gonghe Printing Bureau, Wang Danru from Xiaojingshanfang, Chen Xingsheng and Pu Fenglai from Haizuo Bookstore, and ten other people. The charter was passed on the spot, and officials were elected. Each member began to pay savings of ten yuan. The association aims to connect industry peers and promote savings. The meetings are held every two days on the 17th of the month. Members pay a monthly savings of twenty yuan, with a term of ten years, deposited in six banks. The cost of unnecessary consumption is saved, and the total amount is expected to inspire many to follow suit.

Development of Cuihua National Language Night School

Mr. Li Youzhi, a local writer, has been in the field of education for 30 years and has taught thousands of students, such as the banker Zhang Gongquan, Jing Runshi, the writer Yan Duhe, Yan Esheng, the manufacturer Wu Yunshu, Xue Xingzhong, the lawyer Yan Yinwu, Yu Qijiang, and the educator Yu Qingtang, Chen Jicheng, and others. Last year, he founded Cuihua National Language Night School, divided into ordinary and advanced courses. There are already more than 100 male and female students. Most of the students are staff from various bureaus, banks, foreign firms, and companies. The third round of new student enrollment is coming up. Correspondence courses and composition correspondence classes have been added to facilitate those who are in other places or restricted by their duties. The mailing address is 88 Aijia Alley, Nanshi. The school address is Xizhi Ming School, Hongqiao. It is said that school will start on September 1st and registration is required in advance.

Insurance Association's Request for Exemption from Stamp Duty Not Approved

The Shanghai Insurance Association previously stated that China's insurance industry is still in its infancy, and if it is not developed urgently, it will be difficult to compete with foreign insurance companies in business. Therefore, it specially requested the Ministry of Finance to exempt it from the stamp duty on actual premiums collected to promote it and reduce the burden. It is learned that the association received a reply from the Ministry of Finance yesterday stating that the request for exemption from stamp duty was not approved.

Local News Two Nights Ago, a Woman was Assassinated on Latour Road

Two Gunshots Pierced the Air

A Woman Collapsed in a Pool of Blood

The Woman's Corpse was in a Very Tragic State

No Findings in the Surrounding Area

At 7:40 PM last night, an anonymous shooting occurred in front of the residence of M. Meunier, a French national from the Sino-French Industrial and Commercial Bank, located at 525 Latour Road, French Concession. The victim was a young woman, approximately in her twenties. The details are recorded as follows:

The Location is Extremely Remote

525 Latour Road, French Concession, is the residence of M. Meunier of the Sino-French Industrial and Commercial Bank. The location is extremely remote, at the southernmost end of Latour Road. Every evening, there are very few pedestrians, and except for a small number of Western residences near the road, the rest are barren tombs or connected vegetable fields.

Two Gunshots

At around 7:40 PM last night, just as Mr. Mann was finishing his supper, he was resting indoors, when the servant Yang Xiuyan, a Hebei native, came to bring tea, and suddenly heard a loud noise near the gate on the road. The master and servant heard the noise, and immediately looked at each other and paid attention, listening carefully, but there was no other movement. At first, they suspected that it was a rickshaw tire bursting. About ten minutes later, another shot was heard in the wasteland behind the house.

Collapsed Woman

After the second shot, Mr. Mann realized that it was a gunshot, but there was still no other movement, so he ignored it. After another ten minutes, at about 8:00 PM, Mr. Mann wanted to go to Maple Grove Bridge to meet a friend, so he drove out in his own car. Unexpectedly, as soon as he arrived at the entrance, he saw a woman lying in a pool of blood by the road on the right side of the door.

Shape of the Woman's Corpse

In a state of shock, Mr. Mann immediately turned around and went back into the house, and urgently used the telephone to notify the patrol of Shanzhong Road, which was in charge. The head of the patrol immediately dispatched a western detective along with patrol detectives Su Deshan and Qian Yumin to rush to the scene of the incident. After a detailed examination, they saw that the woman's corpse was about twenty years old, with short hair hanging down to her shoulders, a slightly collapsed nose, wearing a white Indian silk cheongsam, only reaching her knees, black silk stockings, and white silk shoes with embroidered landscape patterns.

A Bullet Through the Head

The skin on the left knee of the corpse's silk stockings was scratched. The right palm was covered with mud and bloodstains. Judging from the situation, it seemed that she had been dragged there by an enemy and tried to struggle and resist without success. A white gauze rope was tied around her right arm, and there was a piece of newspaper containing white gauze and a pair of men's shorts. There were only twenty-five copper coins in the pocket of the shorts, and nothing else. A bullet hole in her right eye socket pierced the back of her head. The situation was very tragic.

Investigation in the Wilderness

After examining the corpse, the detectives went to the back of the house to investigate the trace of the second shot. At that time, it was extremely dark. The reporter, moved by curiosity, also followed the crowd to investigate. Unexpectedly, the back of the house was all wilderness, with several acres of fields, all planted with green eggplant. The southern part was covered with grass up to the ankles, with a solitary grave inside, surrounded by an earth enclosure. In front of the enclosure was a small pond with a circumference of more than forty steps. After searching almost everywhere, there was no trace. They returned to the patrol to report, and notified the Tongren Fuyuantang to carry the corpse to the coroner's office to await examination today.

The Myth of a Maid Resurrecting After Dying from Illness

Lively Streets in the Dark World

Ten Years of Life Extended After Being Pushed and Falling Awake

A maid named Lu, about thirty years old, who worked for a certain family in Anshun Lane, Kandi Road, French New Concession, suddenly fell ill on the 10th of this month and died soon after. At that time, the employer, because the corpse's chest and other parts were still warm and not cold, did not dare to hastily encoffin and bury it, and temporarily set it aside. They also sent a letter to Lu's family to come to Shanghai to handle the matter. This went on for five days. Unexpectedly, Lu suddenly woke up and resurrected. At this time, the employer's whole family was shocked and could not stop. Afterwards, they asked Lu about what happened after death. Lu described the situation after death, saying that after death, she went to a dark world, where there were many vendors, all kinds of goods were available, and there were shops, very lively, especially like the streets of the Yangjian. While walking, she met an old woman who had passed away more than ten years ago, who scolded me sternly and said, "What are you doing here? This is not a place for you to come. You still have more than ten years of Yangshou." After saying this, she stretched out her hand and pushed me to the ground, and I woke up from the shock. The employer and his family were horrified when they heard this. Since then, Lu's illness has been cured, and she has quit her job and returned to her hometown to recuperate with her family.

Lawyer Personality Case Heard Yesterday

Gu Yongquan Filed Counterclaim, Difficult to Reach Settlement

Zou Yu Said There are Many Scoundrels Among Shanghai Lawyers

Wang Chengkuan Asked to Record That He Scolded Me as a Thief

Qu Shunxiang and Zhou Jianren were involved in a criminal lawsuit in the Shanghai District Court due to a dispute over ancestral graves. This led to a conflict between the two lawyers, Wang Chengkuan and Gu Yongquan, who were acting as witnesses when the documents were signed. Gu pointed out that Wang was too unprincipled and was a scoundrel among lawyers. At that time, Judge Shen Xing intervened and said that there should be no public insults in the courtroom. Lawyer Wang Chengkuan, feeling that Gu was also a commissioned lawyer, each seeking the interests of the parties, and should not publicly insult him in court, filed a lawsuit with the court, requesting legal action. The defendant, Gu Yongquan, in addition to defending himself, also filed a counterclaim, stating that the plaintiff, Wang Chengkuan, should not have slandered him in court. Yesterday morning, Presiding Judge Zhao opened the third hearing. The plaintiff, Wang Chengkuan, was represented by lawyer Tao Jiachun, and the defendant, Gu Yongquan, was represented by lawyer Zou Yu. After the judge took his seat, the plaintiff, Wang Chengkuan, first stated the facts of the insult and requested that it be dealt with and ordered that the verdict be published in the newspaper. The defendant, Gu Yongquan, said that because Wang Chengkuan said that on May 26, I offered him a bribe of 2,000 yuan, which he refused, and turned around and accused me, so I said that Lawyer Wang was too unprincipled and made false testimony, and was a scoundrel among lawyers. However, I am a witness, and the dispute with the witness is not an insult. Wang Chengkuan falsely accused me of bribery of 2,000 yuan, but I was in the Special District Court at 2:00 PM that afternoon, appearing in the Shimin Bank fraud case, so I had no time to bribe. This shows that he is slandering my reputation, and I request an investigation. Lawyers Ye Fikang and Jiang Baolian can testify to this, and I request that they be summoned. Wang Chengkuan replied that the defendant has already admitted to public insult, and the case is self-incriminating, so there is no need for Ye Fikang and Jiang Baolian to testify. As for the matter of him offering me 2,000 yuan, it is true that the party, Hua Jingtang, was present and can testify. When I testified at that time, I stated this matter to the judge after the defendant scolded me first. Whether to adopt it or not is the judge's freedom. If it is false testimony, it can also be transferred to the prosecutor's office for investigation by the judge. The defendant should not scold others with insulting words such as unprincipled scoundrel. At this point, the judge asked Tao Jiachun, the lawyer hired by the self-incriminating party, if he had any comments. Lawyer Tao stood up and said that as for this case, the defendant has already admitted to public insult, which is certainly established. However, after this case occurred, this lawyer and Lawyer Jiang Baolian had consulted on a settlement in order to settle the matter. Today we are still in consultation, so the defendant should request an adjournment in order

Repatriation of Overseas Chinese from Japan Continues 86

Chinese Laborers in Nagoya: Due to the economic downturn, Japanese factories are embracing cost-cutting policies, and Chinese laborers employed within these factories are being repatriated one after another. Workers dismissed from various factories in Nagoya's Naka Ward, facing destitution, are being sent back to Shanghai. The first batch includes Wu Hexun, Qiu Yinlu, Chen Dengjin, Qiu Chaomei, Ye Yongshan, Xia Chao, Fei Yisunlu, Lin Qifei, Jin Dengfei, Ren Zizhong, Wu Chaomei, Jiao Ruiren, and others, mostly from Qingtian, Zhejiang. Their return from Japan is in a pitiful state. Two or three more batches of Chinese laborers are scheduled to arrive. Furthermore, a group of individuals who were making a living in the area through skilled trades has also been sent back to Shanghai by the Japanese authorities.

Chinese Merchants in Yokohama: Chinese in Tokyo and Yokohama who were engaged in petty vending, kimono and food businesses, and barbering have already been sent back over 500 li by the Japanese. Now, Chinese from Asakawa Yamashita-cho and Fukagawa in Tokyo, facing destitution, are also being sent back to Shanghai by the Japanese authorities in succession. A group including Liang Zhaozhen, Fang Acun, Le Quansheng, Xiang Zhiqing, Yu Xinfa, Tang Yannan, Zhang Zhongbin, Zheng Baimei, and others, were forced onto a Japanese ship and expelled back to Shanghai.

Shanghai Import and Export Trade 87

Sharp Increase in July

According to a recent survey, the total value of Shanghai's foreign trade in July was 46 million Haikwan taels for imports and 39 million Haikwan taels for exports. Compared with June, imports increased by more than 8 million Haikwan taels and exports increased by more than 5 million taels, an average increase of 14% to 20%. However, compared with the same period last year, imports are still down 5% and exports are down 7%. Since the soaring gold prices, the port's import and export trade has plummeted and declined. The sudden increase in July was unexpected. Based on the current situation, there is hope for the recovery of Shanghai's import and export trade. If the military situation can be settled soon, with the Mid-Autumn Festival approaching, Shanghai's foreign trade will surely develop further.

Guns for the Yixian Warship to be Shipped to Shanghai 88

The construction of the Yixian cruiser, newly built by the Jiangnan Shipyard of the Navy Department, is proceeding actively. The steel plates and framework of the hull have been installed, and the launching ceremony is scheduled for November, with full completion expected in April next year. The cost is estimated at 2 million yuan. The large and small guns to be installed, all ordered from Germany, include over ten 8-inch and 6-inch guns. The cost is no less than 2 million yuan. It is heard that they have been manufactured and will soon be shipped to Shanghai by mail ship in succession.

Funding Issues for the County Government 89

Instructions Received from the Finance Department Yesterday

Regarding the funding issues for the Shanghai County Government, the Shanghai County Finance Bureau received instructions from the Provincial Finance Department yesterday, stating, "For compliance, the Jiangsu Provincial Government's Instruction No. 472 states: 'According to item 14 of the discussion matters at the 319th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee, Committee Member and concurrently Director of the Finance Department, Qi Cai, proposed a plan to address financial difficulties. After deliberation, (1) military police salaries and educational subsidies will be issued as usual; (2) each agency's expenses will be issued at 50% first, to be managed by the agencies themselves, temporarily for August and September; supplements will be issued successively after October; (3) other expenses that can be deferred will be jointly determined by the relevant authorities and reported to the meeting,' etc. In addition to separate communications, a memorandum is issued to the Department for instructing the affiliated departments to comply with the above." Following this, in addition to distributing the information, a memorandum is issued to the Director of the Bureau for compliance, etc.

Pilot Training Institute Re-Urges Pilots of All Ships to Attend Classes 90

The Yangtze River Pilot Training Institute of the Navy Department sent a letter yesterday to the Shanghai Shipping Association and various shipping companies, stating: "Respectfully informing you, according to the Hydrographic Office's forwarded Instruction No. 338 from the Navy Department: 'For your information, the pilot profession is responsible for navigating ships through dangerous waterways, bearing a heavy responsibility. All regulations regarding collision avoidance, temporary warnings, and various signal markers must be clearly understood to ensure appropriate responses. Currently, Yangtze River pilots are only familiar with the river's depth changes, and few are proficient in navigation skills. This is vastly different from the qualifications required of pilots in other countries. The Pilot Examination Regulations will be promulgated soon, stipulating the exclusive use of nationals. If such talent is not cultivated in advance, it may provide grounds for criticism from foreigners. The Training Institute is responsible for guidance and encouragement and should order measures to be taken to promote learning, either by informing the pilot associations or consulting with shipping companies, to carefully guide the pilots, inspire their enthusiasm for learning, and encourage their progress, without allowing them to be sporadic in their studies, lest they miss the course. Report the pilot training situation at any time. This is essential,' etc. Following this, pilot services are inherently related to maritime rights, and also have a great relationship with the business operations of various commercial ships. Deep expertise in navigation is necessary to gain the trust of Chinese and foreign parties. Currently, Chinese pilots lack research in the navigation-related sciences needed, making it difficult to compete with foreigners. To prepare for the implementation of the Yangtze River pilot system, the government has established an institute for training, developing complete pilot talent, and stipulating the exclusive use of nationals, which is intended to consider both the current and future benefits of all pilots. Regarding pilots who cannot attend classes on time due to business reasons, this institute has also taken this into consideration. Therefore, pilots who are often in Shanghai and those who return to Shanghai with ships are required to attend classes on time. This has previously been communicated to your company for reference and to inform the pilots to comply.

Page 14

In accordance with the aforementioned instruction, we respectfully request that your company comply with the spirit of the Ministry's instructions, diligently persuade all employed Yangtze River pilots registered with this institute to strive to learn, attend classes on time, and carefully study navigation skills, so that they may be qualified to take the examination and obtain a formal business license. Please also instruct them not to rely solely on their current experience and become complacent, hindering their studies and missing the examination. This matter concerns the vital interests of each pilot, so please do not hesitate to observe, but strive to make progress and become complete pilot talent, in strict accordance with the Ministry's instructions. We have high expectations. In addition to notifying separately, this letter is to inform you for reference and to inform all pilots to comply. Sincerely, (Another letter to the Pilot Association, content omitted for brevity.)

Request for Postponement of Autonomous Region Division 91

The Beijing and Shanghai Municipal Governments Will Jointly Submit a Request

The Shanghai Municipal Government, noting that after the promulgation of the Municipal Organization Law, the deadline for dividing autonomous regions is imminent, and that Shanghai's area is vast, making the process even more difficult, has specifically requested the Nanjing Municipal Government to send a copy of the various district division procedures for reference. It is now heard that the Beijing Municipal Government has replied to the Shanghai Municipal Government, stating that it is also difficult to complete the task as scheduled, and that the Beijing and Shanghai Municipal Governments plan to jointly submit a request to the National Government to request a postponement.
